        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1],

        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1],

        FROM   (SELECT TOP (2) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name],

            [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash],

            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM [dbo].[T_AdminUserConfig] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[AdminUserId] AS [AdminUserId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_AdminUserRoles] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[RoleId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[AdminUserId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C1] ASC

        [Extent11].[HouseId] AS [HouseId], 
        [Extent11].[Url] AS [Url], 
        [Extent11].[ThumbUrl] AS [ThumbUrl], 
        [Extent11].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime8], 
        [Extent11].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted8], 
        CASE WHEN ([Extent11].[Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM            (SELECT [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent1].[CommunityId] AS [CommunityId], [Extent1].[RoomTypeId] AS [RoomTypeId], [Extent1].[Address] AS [Address], [Extent1].[MonthRent] AS [MonthRent], [Extent1].[StatusId] AS [StatusId], [Extent1].[Area] AS [Area], [Extent1].[DecorateStatusId] AS [DecorateStatusId], [Extent1].[TotalFloorCount] AS [TotalFloorCount], [Extent1].[FloorIndex] AS [FloorIndex], [Extent1].[TypeId] AS [TypeId], [Extent1].[Direction] AS [Direction], [Extent1].[LookableDateTime] AS [LookableDateTime], [Extent1].[CheckinDateTime] AS [CheckinDateTime], [Extent1].[OwnerName] AS [OwnerName], [Extent1].[OwnerPhoneNum] AS [OwnerPhoneNum], [Extent1].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Houses] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE 0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]
            ORDER BY [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] DESC
            OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 10 ROWS ONLY  ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_Communities] AS [Extent2] ON [Limit1].[CommunityId] = [Extent2].[Id]
        INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Regions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent2].[RegionId] = [Extent3].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_Communities] AS [Extent4] ON [Limit1].[CommunityId] = [Extent4].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_Regions] AS [Extent5] ON [Extent4].[RegionId] = [Extent5].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_Cities] AS [Extent6] ON [Extent5].[CityId] = [Extent6].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_IdNames] AS [Extent7] ON [Limit1].[DecorateStatusId] = [Extent7].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_IdNames] AS [Extent8] ON [Limit1].[RoomTypeId] = [Extent8].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_IdNames] AS [Extent9] ON [Limit1].[StatusId] = [Extent9].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_IdNames] AS [Extent10] ON [Limit1].[TypeId] = [Extent10].[Id]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_HousePics] AS [Extent11] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Extent11].[HouseId]
        WHERE ([Extent3].[CityId] = @p__linq__0) AND ([Limit1].[TypeId] = @p__linq__1)
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[CreateDateTime] DESC, [Project1].[Id1] ASC, [Project1].[Id2] ASC, [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[Id3] ASC, [Project1].[Id4] ASC, [Project1].[Id5] ASC, [Project1].[Id6] ASC, [Project1].[Id7] ASC, [Project1].[Id8] ASC, [Project1].[Id9] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC
